### [120] [Compact vs. Scattered: Suitability of Southern 6.7GHz Methanol Masers for VLBI astrometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16998)
*Lucas J. Hyland,Simon P. Ellingsen,Mark J. Reid*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 6.7 GHz甲醇脉泽与大质量年轻恒星相关，适合用于天体测量研究。通过长基线阵列观测187个南半天区源，发现69个适合VLBI天体测量的致密强脉泽源。脉泽致密性与银河系位置相关，近臂源更致密，远臂或银心区域则因散射展宽而较弥散，这对利用远距离脉泽进行银河系天体测量有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别适合进行高精度天体测量（如三角视差测距）的6.7 GHz甲醇脉泽源，并研究其空间分布特征和物理条件对观测适用性的影响。

Method: 使用Long Baseline Array对187个南半天区的6.7 GHz甲醇脉泽源进行甚长基线干涉测量观测，分析脉泽斑点的致密性和强度，评估其作为天体测量目标的可行性，并探讨其在银河系中的位置与致密性之间的关系。

Result: 在187个源中识别出69个具有足够致密和强烈脉泽斑点的候选体，适合作为当前仪器下的VLBI天体测量目标；发现脉泽致密性随银河系位置变化，近螺旋臂源更致密，远距离或银心区域源更弥散，归因于散射展宽效应。

Conclusion: 脉泽源的观测适用性受其在银河系中位置的影响，散射展宽是限制远距离脉泽天体测量精度的重要因素，未来选择目标时需考虑该效应。

Abstract: The 6.7~GHz methanol maser transition is exclusively associated with young,
high-mass stars and represents a potential target for astrometric studies,
including accurate determination of their distance through trigonometric
parallax measurements. There are more than 1000 known 6.7~GHz methanol maser
sources in the Milky Way; however, not all are suitable targets for astrometric
measurements. We have used the Long Baseline Array to observe 187 southern
6.7~GHz methanol masers and identify 69 sources with one or more maser spots
that are sufficiently compact and intense to be suitable targets for very long
baseline interferometry astrometry with current instruments. Maser compactness
appears to be a strong function of Galactic position, with masers that are
likely in nearby spiral arms being more compact, while those associated with
distant arms or the central Galactic region being less compact - a relationship
we associate with scatter broadening. This has implications for astrophysical
masers, especially distant ones employed for Galactic astrometry.

### [121] [Protostars at Subsolar Metallicity: First Detection of Large Solid-state Complex Organic Molecules in the Large Magellanic Cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17138)
*Marta Sewiło,Will R. M. Rocha,Martijn van Gelder,Maria Gabriela Navarro,Steven B. Charnley,Miwha Jin,Joana M. Oliveira,Jacco Th. van Loon,Logan Francis,Jennifer Wiseman,Remy Indebetouw,C. -H. Rosie Chen,Roya Hamedani Golshan,Danna Qasim*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 首次在大麦哲伦云中的原恒星ST6周围冰中探测到多种复杂有机分子，包括乙酸，并发现其与银河系原恒星在冰丰度上的差异可能源于金属丰度和紫外辐射的不同。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究低金属丰度和强紫外辐射环境下恒星形成区的物理与化学特性，模拟早期宇宙条件下的星际化学过程。

Method: 利用詹姆斯·韦布空间望远镜的中红外仪器对ST6进行4.9-27.9微米光谱观测，结合实验室冰光谱数据，使用ENIIGMA拟合工具或局部连续谱方法分析6.8-8.4微米范围内的光谱以确定冰壳层的组成和分子丰度。

Conclusion: 低金属丰度和强紫外辐射显著影响复杂有机分子的形成与丰度，表明早期宇宙条件下星际化学可能与银河系内有所不同，需更多实验室光谱数据以提升对原恒星光谱的解析能力。

Abstract: We present the results of James Webb Space Telescope observations of the
protostar ST6 in the Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC) with the Medium Resolution
Spectrograph of the Mid-Infrared Instrument (4.9-27.9 $\mu$m). Characterized by
one-third to half-solar metallicity and strong UV radiation fields, the
environment of the LMC allows us to study the physics and chemistry of
star-forming regions under the conditions similar to those at earlier
cosmological epochs. We detected five icy complex organic molecules (COMs):
methanol (CH$_3$OH), acetaldehyde (CH$_3$CHO), ethanol (CH$_3$CH$_2$OH), methyl
formate (HCOOCH$_3$), and acetic acid (CH$_3$COOH). This is the first
conclusive detection of CH$_3$COOH ice in an astrophysical context, and
CH$_3$CHO, CH$_3$CH$_2$OH, and HCOOCH$_3$ ices are the first secure detections
outside the Galaxy and in a low-metallicity environment. We address the
presence of glycolaldehyde (HOCH$_2$CHO, a precursor of biomolecules), an
isomer of HCOOCH$_3$ and CH$_3$COOH, but its detection is inconclusive. ST6's
spectrum is also rich in simple ices: H$_2$O, CO$_2$, CH$_4$, SO$_2$, H$_2$CO,
HCOOH, OCN$^{-}$, HCOO$^{-}$, NH$_3$, and NH$_4^{+}$. We obtain the composition
and molecular abundances in the icy dust mantles by fitting the spectrum in the
6.8-8.4 $\mu$m range with a large sample of laboratory ice spectra using the
ENIIGMA fitting tool or the local continuum method. We found differences in the
simple and COM ice abundances with respect to H$_2$O ice between ST6 and
Galactic protostars that likely reflect differences in metallicity and UV flux.
More laboratory ice spectra of COMs are needed to better reconstruct the
observed infrared spectra of protostars.

</details>


### [122] [Photoionization Modeling of Planetary Nebulae in the Galactic Bulge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17265)
*N. Aksaker,A. Demirci,N. Erzincan,A. Akyuz*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用Cloudy代码对银河系核球中的124个行星状星云进行了光致电离模型分析，得出了中心恒星的有效温度、光度、电离区半径及元素丰度等关键参数，并与观测数据对比，提供了迄今为止最全面的行星状星云光致电离模型结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了深入理解银河系核球中行星状星云的物理性质及其演化过程，需要通过光致电离模型系统性地推导中心恒星和星云的参数。

Method: 使用Cloudy代码对124个行星状星云进行光致电离建模，推导中心恒星有效温度、光度、电离区半径、元素丰度等参数，并与观测数据比较，评估模型拟合优度（χ²），结合赫罗图分析恒星演化轨迹。

Result: 中心恒星有效温度峰值约为100,000 K，光度集中在~3,000 L⊙；电离区半径为0.003–0.31 pc，星云直径平均比可见光观测大7%；元素丰度整体一致（差异<0.5 dex），但S、N、Cl存在显著变化；模型与观测总体吻合良好（尤其是Cl/H），但He/H和S/H存在明显偏差；χ²值差异较大，高值与WISE测光数据偏差相关；中心星前身星质量为0.8–4.2 M⊙，最终质量为0.53–0.87 M⊙，表明显著质量损失；后AGB年龄为150–20,000年，多数处于中等演化阶段。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了目前最全面的银河系核球星云光致电离模型，揭示了中心恒星的演化路径及星云的物理化学特性，对理解行星状星云的形成、演化及质量损失过程具有重要意义。

Abstract: In this study, we present the results of photoionization modeling for 124
planetary nebulae (PNe) in the Galactic bulge. Utilizing the {\scshape cloudy}
code, we derived the effective temperatures (T$_{eff}$) of the central stars,
with a peak distribution around $\sim$ 100,000 K, and luminosities clustering
around $\sim$ 3,000 L$\odot$. The inner radii of the ionized regions range from
0.003 to 0.31 pc, with nebula diameters varying from 1.8" to 34", averaging 7\%
larger than the observed visible diameters. Elemental abundances for Helium,
Nitrogen, Oxygen, Neon, Sulphur, Chlorine and Argon relative to hydrogen
derived from the models show consistency within 0.5 dex, with notable
variations in Sulphur, Nitrogen, and Chlorine. The study also compares
elemental abundances from photoionization models with previous observations,
showing overall good agreement, particularly for Cl/H, but notable
discrepancies in He/H and S/H ratios. The models' goodness of fit, quantified
by $\chi^{2}$ values, varies widely, with higher values linked to discrepancies
in WISE photometric data. The evolutionary tracks of the central stars from H-R
diagrams suggest progenitor masses ranging from 0.8 to 4.2 $M_\odot$ and
progenitor final masses between 0.53 and 0.87 $M_\odot$, indicating significant
mass loss during evolution. These PNe have post-AGB ages ranging from 150 to
20,000 years, consistent with the Galactic PNe distribution. Most of the PNe
are in an intermediate evolutionary stage with larger nebular sizes. Our
results provide the most comprehensive photoionization modeling to date, with
key implications for central stars of PNe, gas, and dust.

</details>


### [123] [Impact of Jet Density on Intracluster Medium Heating in Self-Regulated AGN Feedback Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17518)
*Tzu-Wei Tsai,Hsiang-Yi Karen Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究通过三维流体动力学模拟探讨了活动星系核（AGN）喷流密度对星系团中加热效率的影响，发现较轻的喷流虽然影响范围更广，但整体加热效率较低，且冷气体分布显著影响加热效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AGN反馈中喷流性质对加热效率的影响，尤其是喷流密度在调节星系团内介质热平衡中的作用尚不明确。

Method: 采用三维流体动力学模拟，构建类似英仙座星系团的模型，比较单喷流与自调节模型下不同密度喷流对气泡演化和介质热平衡的影响。

Result: 较轻的喷流形成更球形的气泡，易被冷气体偏转，实现更各向同性的能量沉积，但整体加热效率较低，需要更高的平均喷流功率来维持自调节；较重的喷流加热效率更高；冷气体的分布和数量显著影响加热效果。

Conclusion: 喷流密度是AGN反馈中的关键参数，未来研究需引入磁场、粘度和宇宙射线等物理过程，以实现与观测的更真实对比。

Abstract: Active galactic nucleus (AGNs) feedback is widely accepted as the key
mechanism to suppress cooling flows in galaxy clusters. However, the dependence
of heating efficiency on jet properties is not fully understood. In this work,
we present three-dimensional hydrodynamic simulations of a Perseus-like
cluster, including both single-jet and self-regulated models, to investigate
how jet density affects bubble evolution and the thermal balance of the
intracluster medium. Our results confirm previous findings that lighter jets
inflate more spherical bubbles and are more easily deflected by cold gas,
enabling isotropic energy deposition throughout the cluster core. However,
despite their broader spatial impact, lighter jets display lower overall
heating efficiency, requiring higher average jet power to maintain
self-regulation compared to heavier jets. We also find that the distribution
and amount of cold gas significantly influence the effectiveness of jet
heating. These results highlight jet density as a critical parameter in AGN
feedback and emphasize the need to incorporate additional physical processes
such as magnetic fields, viscosity, and cosmic rays in future studies for
realistic comparisons with observations.

</details>


### [124] [MEGADES: MEGARA galaxy disc evolution survey. Ionised gas diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17565)
*M. Chamorro-Cazorla,A. Gil de Paz,A. Castillo-Morales,A. Camps-Fariña,J. Gallego,E. Carrasco,J. Iglesias-Páramo,R. Cedazo,M. L. García-Vargas,S. Pascual,N. Cardiel,A. Pérez-Calpena,P. Gómez-Álvarez,I. Martínez-Delgado,C. Catalán-Torrecilla,J. Zamorano*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本论文利用MEGADES巡天数据研究了43个星系的电离气体性质和金属丰度梯度，使用MEGARA仪器的高分辨率光谱分析BPT图及其随半径和H-alpha速度弥散的变化，提出了一种新的基于[N II]/H-alpha速度弥散比的诊断方法来区分AGN、激波和H II区的作用。通过改进H II区的选择，获得了可靠的氧丰度估计，发现大多数星系金属丰度梯度平缓，尤其在低丰度快速旋转星系中，而高丰度星系则呈现轻微负梯度，并讨论了星系风对丰度梯度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系中电离气体的来源（如AGN、激波、H II区）及其对金属丰度分布的影响，特别是金属丰度梯度如何反映星系演化过程中的气体流动和化学演化。

Method: 利用MEGARA仪器的高光谱（R ~ 6000）和空间分辨率（0.62角秒）数据，应用经典的BPT诊断（[N II]和[S II]变体），分析其随半径和H-alpha速度弥散的变化；提出基于[N II]6584与H-alpha线速度弥散比的新诊断方法；使用N2指标估算氧丰度并分析金属丰度梯度。

Result: 许多区域表现出激波特征发射，位于H II与AGN区间；新方法有助于更准确识别H II区；大多数星系金属丰度梯度接近零，尤其是低丰度快速旋转星系（平均斜率0.005 dex/Re，弥散0.42）；高丰度（>8.37 dex）快速旋转星系呈现负梯度（均值-0.68 dex/Re）；整个样本平均梯度为-0.03 dex/Re，弥散0.77。

Conclusion: 星系中广泛存在激波电离作用；改进的H II区选择提升了丰度测量可靠性；金属丰度梯度总体较平缓，支持星系风等反馈机制在调控化学演化中的重要作用。

Abstract: We present the ionised gas properties and metallicity gradients of 43
galaxies observed by the MEGADES survey. Using the MEGARA (Multi-Espectrografo
en GTC de Alta Resolucion para Astronomia) instrument, our data combine
relatively high spectral (R ~ 6000) and spatial (0.62 arcsec) resolution to
study the ionised gas through classic BPT diagnostics in the [N II] and [S II]
variants. We examine how these diagrams vary with radius and with the velocity
dispersion of the H-alpha line, and we propose a new diagnostic based on the
ratio between the velocity dispersions of the [N II] 6584 and H-alpha lines to
disentangle the relative roles of AGN, shocks and H II regions. Many regions,
regardless of galactocentric distance, show shock-like emission, inferred from
their line ratios (high [N II]6584/H-alpha and intermediate [O III]5007/H-beta)
and their location between H II and AGN regimes. This improved selection of H
II-like regions enables robust oxygen abundance estimates using the N2
indicator. Most galaxies show negligible metallicity gradients, especially
low-abundance (<8.37 dex) fast rotators, with an average slope of 0.005 dex
Re^-1 and a dispersion of 0.42 dex Re^-1. Above 8.37 dex, fast rotators display
mildly negative gradients (mean -0.68 dex Re^-1, dispersion 0.93). For the full
MEGADES sample, the mean gradient is -0.03 dex Re^-1 with a dispersion of 0.77.
We discuss the implications for the influence of galactic winds on abundance
gradients.

*Taylor Spoo,Katelyn Thomas,Ellie "Kaleo" Toguchi-Tani,Jonah Otto,Natalie Myers,Jamie Tayar,Jessica S. Schonhut-Stasik,Matthew Shetrone,Alessa Ibrahim Wiggins,John Donor,Peter M. Frinchaboy*

Method: 结合原有的开放星团校准样本与四个球状星团（47 Tuc、M 71、M 4、M 5）的数据，建立并扩展[C/N]丰度比与恒星年龄之间的经验关系，并在APOGEE DR17红巨星样本中进行验证，同时与星震学测得的年龄（APOKASC、APO-K2）进行比较。

Conclusion: [C/N]丰度比可被可靠地用于估算银河系不同区域（包括贫金属区域）演化场星的年龄，特别是在APOGEE DR17数据中具有统一适用性。

Abstract: In the coming years, detailed chemical abundances from large-scale
high-resolution spectroscopic surveys will become available for vast numbers of
stars across the Milky Way. Previous work has suggested that abundance ratios
from these spectra can allow us to estimate ages from a large number of stars.
These data will be leveraged to calibrate chemical clocks to age-date field
stars, as reliable stellar ages remain elusive. In this work, we extended our
empirical relationship between stellar age and their carbon-to-nitrogen ([C/N])

combining the original open cluster calibration sample and four globular

a chemical clock for evolved field stars to investigate not only regions within
the metal rich disk, but also more metal-poor regions of our Galaxy. We have
established the [C/N]-age relationship for APOGEE DR17 red giant stars, that
have experienced the first dredge up but have not yet undergone any
extra-mixing, in clusters usable for ages between $8.62 \leq \log(Age[{\rm
yr}]) \leq 10.13$ and for metallicites of $-1.2\leq[Fe/H]\leq+0.3$. This
relationship can be uniformly applied to these stars within the APOGEE DR17
sample. This measured [C/N]-age APOGEE DR17 relationship is also shown to be
consistent with stellar ages derived from asterosiesmic results of APOKASC and
APO-K2.

Abstract: The earliest assembly of the Milky Way (MW) remains poorly understood, yet
the spatial, chemical, and kinematic properties of its most metal-poor stars
provide a unique fossil record of its proto-Galaxy phase. Understanding how
this ancient component formed is essential for linking near-field Galactic
archaeology to high-redshift galaxy evolution. We construct the currently
largest 3-D map of inner-Galaxy metal-poor giants by combining several
narrow/medium-band photometric surveys, reaching metallicities down to
[Fe/H]$\sim-$3.5. Comparing observational data with Auriga 18 (Au18) from the

local fossil records with future studies of early star-forming galaxies.

### [127] [Increased molecular gas velocity dispersion and star formation efficiency in barred galaxy centres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17768)
*Jennifer M. Laing,Christine D. Wilson*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用PHANGS-ALMA巡天的高分辨率CO(2-1)数据和依赖速度弥散的α_CO转换因子分析分子气体表面密度、速度弥散、恒星形成率和耗尽时间。

Result: 发现棒星系中心的分子气体表面密度、速度弥散更高，耗尽时间更短；即使排除AGN影响，差异仍显著；速度弥散随恒星形成率增加而上升，暗示棒驱动的气体流入增强了非圆周运动。

dispersions in the centres of barred galaxies compared to unbarred galaxies. We
explore central molecular gas using published high resolution (150 pc)
measurements of CO$(2-1)$ from the PHANGS-ALMA survey and a new velocity
dispersion-dependent prescription for the CO-to-H$_{2}$ conversion factor
$\alpha_{\rm{CO}}$. Comparisons of the molecular gas surface density, velocity
dispersion, star formation rate, and depletion time reveal that these
quantities are different in the centres of barred and unbarred galaxies. Gas
depletion times are found to be shorter in barred galaxy centres. Even when we
control for the presence of an AGN, the velocity dispersion and depletion time
are found to be statistically different between barred and unbarred galaxy
centres. The higher velocity dispersion suggests extra non-circular motions,
possibly due to the inflow of gas along the bar, that are not constant but must
increase as the star formation rate increases.

### [128] [The baryonic mass-size relation of galaxies. I. A dichotomy in star-forming galaxy disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17770)
*Zichen Hua,Federico Lelli,Enrico Di Teodoro,Stacy McGaugh,James Schombert*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究利用SPARC数据库分析了星系的重子质量-半径关系，发现高表面密度（HSD）和低表面密度（LSD）星系在重子质量与尺寸平面上形成两个明显不同的序列，揭示了两类恒星形成星系的不同演化路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究通常分别考虑恒星或气体的质量-尺寸关系，本研究旨在通过总重子质量和重子半质量半径，全面理解星系的结构与演化差异。

Method: 使用SPARC数据库中的星系样本，分析其总重子质量（M_bar）与重子半质量半径（R_50,bar）之间的关系，并区分HSD和LSD星系的分布特征。

Result: 发现HSD星系（星体主导）的质量-尺寸关系斜率接近1，表明较轻的旋涡星系更致密；LSD星系（气体主导）斜率接近2，意味着平均表面密度近似恒定。该二分性在Tully-Fisher关系中不显著，但在角动量关系中有所体现，主要由相同重子质量下R_50,bar的变化驱动。

Conclusion: 重子质量-尺寸关系是区分不同类型星系并研究其演化的最有效经验工具，揭示了HSD和LSD星系在恒星形成效率和结构演化上的根本差异。

Abstract: The mass-size relations of galaxies are generally studied considering only
stars or only gas separately. Here we study the baryonic mass-size relation of
galaxies from the SPARC database, using the total baryonic mass ($M_{\rm bar}$)
and the baryonic half-mass radius ($R_{\rm 50, bar}$). We find that SPARC
galaxies define two distinct sequences in the $M_{\rm bar} - R_{\rm 50, bar}$
plane: one that formed by high-surface-density (HSD), star-dominated, Sa-to-Sc
galaxies, and one by low-surface-density (LSD), gas-dominated, Sd-to-dI
galaxies. The $M_{\rm bar} - R_{\rm 50, bar}$ relation of LSD galaxies has a
slope close to 2, pointing to a constant average surface density, whereas that
of HSD galaxies has a slope close to 1, indicating that less massive spirals
are progressively more compact. Our results point to the existence of two types
of star-forming galaxies that follow different evolutionary paths: HSD disks
are very efficient in converting gas into stars, perhaps thanks to the
efficient formation of non-axisymmetric structures (bars and spiral arms),
whereas LSD disks are not. The HSD-LSD dichotomy is absent in the baryonic
Tully-Fisher relation ($M_{\rm bar}$ versus flat circular velocity $V_{\rm f}$)
but moderately seen in the angular-momentum relation (approximately $M_{\rm
bar}$ versus $V_{\rm f}\times R_{\rm 50, bar}$), so it is driven by variations
in $R_{\rm 50, bar}$ at fixed $M_{\rm bar}$. This fact suggests that the
baryonic mass-size relation is the most effective empirical tool to distinguish
different galaxy types and study their evolution.

</details>


### [129] [Resolving the dusty star-forming galaxy GN20 at z=4.055 with NOEMA and JWST: A similar distribution of stars, gas and dust despite distinct apparent profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17804)
*Leindert A. Boogaard,Fabian Walter,Axel Weiss,Luis Colina,Jacqueline Hodge,Arjan Bik,Alejandro Crespo Gómez,Emanuele Daddi,Georgios E. Magdis,Romain A. Meyer,Göran Östlin*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 高分辨率NOEMA和JWST观测揭示了z=4.055星暴星系GN20中广泛分布的尘埃发射，表明其经历了近期并合事件，且尘埃与分子气体分布受辐射转移效应影响显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高红移星暴星系GN20中的尘埃与恒星、分子气体的空间分布关系，探讨星暴活动的驱动机制及尘埃与气体分布差异的原因。

Method: 结合NOEMA的1.1 mm连续谱观测与JWST/NIRCam、MIRI成像，进行高分辨率多波段形态分析，并通过自洽的辐射转移模型拟合积分和分辨的CO与尘埃发射。

Result: 发现GN20的尘埃发射延伸至约14 kpc，呈中心不对称且致密核区最亮；总尘埃质量为$M_{dust}=5.7^{+0.8}_{-0.6}\times 10^{9}$ Msun，分子气体质量为$M_{mol}=2.9^{+0.4}_{-0.3}\times10^{11}$ Msun，尘气比约为50；尘埃与恒星、气体有共同中心但表面亮度剖面不同，该差异可由辐射转移效应解释。

Conclusion: GN20的星暴活动高度延展，可能由近期并合触发；尽管气体与尘埃的表观径向分布不同，但其真实质量分布相似，强调在比较不同示踪物时需考虑辐射转移效应。

Abstract: We present high-resolution (0.13"-0.23") NOEMA observations of the dust
continuum emission at 1.1 mm (rest-frame 220 micron) and JWST/NIRCam and MIRI
imaging of the z=4.055 starburst galaxy GN20. The sensitive NOEMA imaging at
1.6 kpc resolution reveals extended dust emission, ~14 kpc in diameter (r_e~2.5
kpc, b/a=0.5), that is centrally asymmetric and clumpy. The dust emission is as
extended as the stellar emission and the molecular gas traced by CO(2-1), with
a common center, and is brightest in the strongly-obscured nuclear part of the
galaxy. Approximately one-third of the total dust emission emerges from the
nucleus and the most prominent clump to the south, and (only) 60% from the
central 3.5x1.5 kpc (0.5"-0.2"), implying that the starburst is very extended.
The combined JWST and NOEMA morphology suggests GN20 experienced a recent
interaction or merger, likely invigorating the starburst. The radial surface
brightness profiles of the molecular gas and near-IR stellar emission are
similar, while in contrast, the dust emission appears significantly more
concentrated. Through self-consistent radiative transfer modeling of the
integrated and resolved CO and dust emission, we derive an
$M_{mol}=2.9^{+0.4}_{-0.3}\times10^{11}$ Msun with
$\alpha_{CO}=2.8^{+0.5}_{-0.3}$. We find that the extended dust implies a lower
global dust optical depth than previously reported, but a high dust mass of
$M_{dust}=5.7^{+0.8}_{-0.6}\times 10^{9}$ Msun and gas-to-dust ratio of ~50.
Furthermore, we show the distinct apparent radial profiles of the gas and dust
can be explained purely by radiative transfer effects and the observations are
consistent with the gas and dust mass being similarly distributed throughout
the starburst. The latter highlights the importance of accounting for radiative
transfer effects when comparing molecular gas and dust distributions from
different tracers.

</details>

### [130] [One-loop Corrected Holographic Shear Viscosity to Entropy Density Ratio at Low Temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16100)
*Leopoldo A. Pando Zayas,Jingchao Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了近极端黑洞中由Schwarzian模式主导的量子涨落及其对引力路径积分中一环修正的影响，特别是在低温下这些修正如何超越半经典结果。通过AdS/CFT对应，作者探讨了这些涨落在近极端渐进AdS₄黑洞膜中的影响，发现剪切引力涨落与一个准零模在一环水平上耦合，导致低温下剪切粘度与熵密度比值违反了已知界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解近极端黑洞在低温下的热力学行为，特别是量子涨落如何影响其物理性质，并检验AdS/CFT框架下输运系数界限的有效性。

Method: 利用有效作用量描述近极端黑洞喉部区域的量子涨落，计算引力路径积分中的一环修正，并分析剪切引力涨落与准零模的耦合对延迟格林函数的影响。

Result: 发现在一环水平上剪切引力涨落与准零模存在耦合，这种耦合改变了延迟格林函数的行为，导致低温下剪切粘度与熵密度之比违反了η/s ≥ 1/(4π)的界限。

Conclusion: 近极端黑洞中的量子涨落显著影响其低能输运性质，在低温下可导致剪切粘度与熵密度比值低于传统界限，提示需重新审视强耦合系统中输运界限的普适性。

Abstract: Near-extremal black holes are known to contain strong quantum fluctuations in
their near-horizon near-AdS$_2$ throat region governed by an effective action
that includes Schwarzian modes. These fluctuations lead to one-loop corrections
in the gravitational path integral that are essential in understanding the
thermodynamics of near-extremal black holes at low temperatures where they
become more dominant that the semi-classical answer. We explore the
implications of these quantum fluctuations for near-extremal asymptotically
AdS$_4$ black branes in the context of the AdS/CFT correspondence. We note that
at one-loop level there is a coupling of the shear gravitational fluctuations
to one of the would-be zero modes. This coupling affects the retarded Green's
function in a way that leads to a low temperature violation of the shear
viscosity to entropy density bound.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用弦-Carroll展开方法，将弦作用量和拉回场按有效光速的幂次展开，用于研究近视界区域的弦动力学。

Result: 分类了弦解族的一般特征，并揭示了一些新的特性。

Conclusion: 弦-Carroll展开为研究非极端BTZ黑洞近视界区域的弦动力学提供了自然且有效的框架。

Abstract: The BTZ black hole provides a tractable (2+1)-dimensional example for
investigating string dynamics in curved spacetime. However, a systematic and
robust analysis of the solution space of strings in the near-horizon region of

### [132] [Phases of Supersymmetric Ground States in $AdS_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16274)
*Harold Jones,Vineeth Krishna,Finn Larsen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了AdS₄×S⁷超引力中BPS黑洞及其基态的相图，发现当R电荷差异超过阈值时，两组分构型（核心黑洞+电荷气体）主导超共形指数，并通过欧几里得路径积分揭示其不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超对称背景下不同电荷区域中基态的构成，以及超共形指数如何反映BPS黑洞与多组分配置之间的竞争。

Method: 通过构建超引力中的相图，结合超共形指数分析和欧几里得路径积分方法，研究不同边界条件下的鞍点主导行为。

Result: BPS黑洞仅在满足非线性约束时存在；当R电荷差异较大时，两组分配置主导指数；路径积分在电荷悬殊时不稳定，而KSW判据无法探测此现象。

Conclusion: 基态结构依赖于电荷分布，大R电荷差异下两体构型取代纯BPS黑洞成为主导，揭示了现有判据的局限性。

Abstract: We construct the phase diagram of supersymmetric ground states in
AdS$_4\times S^7$ supergravity. BPS black holes exist only when the conserved
charges satisfy a certain non-linear constraint. For other charge sectors, we
propose two component configurations comprised of a core black hole that
carries macroscopic entropy, and a gas that carries a macroscopic fraction of
the charge. The superconformal index counts ground states only modulo a linear
constraint on the charges. Each index line includes a pure BPS black hole but
we find that, when differences between R-charge exceed a certain threshold, the
index is dominated by a two component configuration. We illuminate this result
by studying the gravitational path integral in Euclidean signature, as function
of supersymmetric boundary conditions. We find that a pure BPS black hole
saddle dominates the index when the R-charges are comparable, but not when they
differ sufficiently. The region where the Euclidean path integral becomes
unstable is precisely where two component configurations dominate the index. We
show that the KSW criteria are insensitive to this instability.

### [133] [Five W-boson amplitude = near-null decagon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16471)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索N=4超杨-米尔斯理论库仑分支上散射振幅的结构及其与重算符关联函数之间的对偶关系，扩展此前在四W玻色子和Sudakov形式因子中发现的对偶性至五点情形。

Method: 从六维N=(1,1)超杨-米尔斯理论出发，通过非零额外维度动量降维至四维，计算五W玻色子振幅在近质量壳极限下的双圈贡献，利用现代解析费曼积分技术，并结合近光锥极限分析其与decagon关联函数的对偶性。

Result: 确认了红外对数的指数化行为，提出了五点振幅的全阶猜想表达式，并在近光锥极限下验证了其与五点重BPS算符关联函数（decagon）的平方根的一致性，支持了新的库仑振幅/重关联函数对偶。

Conclusion: 五W玻色子振幅在近质量壳极限下表现出良好的红外结构和对偶性质，进一步证实了库仑分支振幅与重BPS算符关联函数之间存在普适的对偶关系。

Abstract: We study a five-leg scattering amplitude on the special Coulomb branch of
planar N=4 super Yang-Mills theory. We reach this point of the moduli space of
scalar vacuum expectation values by considering six-dimensional N=(1,1) super
Yang-Mills theory and reducing it down to four space-time dimensions with
extra-dimensional momenta being nonvanishing. This branch is characterized by
massive external W-bosons and massless internal gluons propagating in loops. We
analyze the five W-boson amplitude in the kinematics when their masses are much
smaller than all Mandelstam-like invariants. This is what we dub the near
mass-shell limit. We perform calculations to two-loop order in 't Hooft
coupling, making use of recent advances in analytic calculations of required
Feynman integrals. Our findings confirm exponentiation of infrared logarithms
and enable us to conjecture a concise all-order expression for the amplitude in
question. We further analyze its duality to the `square root' of a five-point
correlation function of infinitely-heavy half-BPS operators, known as the
decagon. By considering the near-null limit for inter-operators distances, we
verify that the two objects coincide. This observation corroborates the novel
Coulomb amplitudes/heavy correlator duality previously observed for four
W-boson amplitudes and Sudakov form factors.

### [134] [Localization mechanism of the Kalb-Ramond field on brane with codimension-two](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16491)
*Yong-Tao Lu,Heng Guo,Qun Wei,Bing Wei*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在具有余维数2的膜上Kalb-Ramond（KR）场的局域化问题，通过一般Kaluza-Klein分解，分析了不同额外维度构型下4D场的局域化行为，并发现引入背景标量耦合后，所有四个4D场均可被局域化，且可能存在共振KK模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨闭弦理论中质量为零的2-形式KR场在高维膜上的局域化机制，理解其在低维有效理论中的实现方式。

Method: 采用一般的Kaluza-Klein分解方法，将六维KR场展开为四维KR场、两个四维矢量场和一个四维标量场，并在不同额外维度构型（R1×R1与R1×S1）下研究各场的局域化特性；进一步引入背景标量耦合以改善局域化条件。

Result: 在R1×R1构型下仅四维标量场可局域化；在R1×S1构型下，一个四维矢量场和标量场可同时局域化且标量质量为零；引入标量耦合后，在t>v²/12条件下所有四个场均可局域化，并可能出现共振KK模式。

Conclusion: 额外维度的拓扑结构和背景标量耦合对KR场在膜上的局域化起关键作用，特定条件下可实现完整低维有效理论的构建。

Abstract: The $2$-form Kalb-Ramond (KR) field, together with the metric tensor and
dilaton, arises as one of the massless excitation mode of a closed string.
Subsequently, this field plays an important role in both string theory and
field theory. In this paper, we investigate the localization of the KR field on
the brane with codimension-2. A general Kaluza-Klein (KK) decomposition is
adopted, wherein the six-dimensional KR field is expanded into one
four-dimensional (4D) KR field, two 4D vector fields, and one 4D scalar field.
Then, for the case of the extra dimensions $\mathcal{R}_1\times\mathcal{R}_1$,
only the 4D scalar field can be localized on the brane. In contrast, for the
case of extra dimensions $\mathcal{R}_1\times\mathcal{S}_1$, one 4D vector
field and the 4D scalar field can be localized on the brane at the same time.
In both cases, the mass of the 4D scalar field remains zero. Next, we examine
the localization of the KR field within a specific six-dimensional brane model
with extra dimensions $\mathcal{R}_1\times\mathcal{S}_1$. By introducing the
background scalar coupling, we show that the 4D KR field, along with the other
three 4D fields, can be localized on the brane under the condition of the
coupling parameter $t>v^2/12$. Additionally in this case, for both the 4D KR
field and the one 4D vector field which acquires its mass from the non-compact
extra dimension, the resonant KK modes could exist near the origin of this
extra dimension.

</details>


### [135] [On Time-Evolution in Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.16543)
*Lasha Berezhiani,Gia Dvali,Otari Sakhelashvili*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论的BRST不变量子化框架下，推导出引力体哈密顿量的一个显式BRST精确算符恒等式，表明其可表示为BRST电荷与时间幽灵场的反对易子，并阐明该形式对物理关联函数的时间重参数化作用，同时论证了该精确性并不导致时间演化或散射振幅的平凡化。

Method: 采用BRST不变的广义相对论量子化方法，通过算符恒等式推导并分析体哈密顿量的BRST精确性及其边界项贡献。

Result: 得到了体哈密顿量作为BRST电荷与时间幽灵场反对易子的显式表达式，揭示了其对物理关联函数的时间重参数化作用，并证明该精确性不导致动力学演化的平凡结果。

Conclusion: 尽管体哈密顿量是BRST精确的，但它仍能非平庸地驱动引力背景和体关联函数的时间演化，且散射振幅保持非平凡，说明该结构具有物理一致性。

Abstract: We derive an explicit BRST-exact operator identity for the bulk Hamiltonian
in quantum gravity, working within a BRST-invariant quantization of General
Relativity, treated as a low-energy effective field theory. We show that, up to
a boundary term, the Hamiltonian can be written elegantly as the anticommutator
of the BRST charge and the temporal ghost field. This form makes manifest that
the Hamiltonian flow acts as a time-reparameterization on the correlation
functions of the physical degrees of freedom. We demonstrate that the
BRST-exactness of the bulk Hamiltonian does not trivialize the time evolution
of gravitational backgrounds or bulk correlators, nor does it trivialize
scattering amplitudes.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更高效地处理广义相对论和二次引力模型中的费曼规则，解决原有工具在鬼粒子-引力子相互作用和规范固定方面的不足，并引入多项式形式的变量以简化计算。

Method: 改进了BRST形式化在广义相对论和二次引力中的实现，引入高导数规范固定项，并实现了Cheung-Remmen变量的费曼规则，同时优化了软件包的用户接口和功能。

Result: 获得了一组有限的鬼粒子与引力子相互作用规则，实现了对Cheung-Remmen变量的完整支持，并增强了FeynGrav的实用性与易用性。

Conclusion: 新版本的FeynGrav显著提升了引力相关理论计算的效率与灵活性，为研究者提供了更强大的工具支持。

Abstract: We present the new version of FeynGrav, a package that provides a set of
tools to work with Feynman rules for gravity models. The new version addresses
two principal issues and includes changes that improve user experience.
Firstly, we present a more sophisticated implementation of the BRST formalism
for general relativity and quadratic gravity, which results in a finite set of
interaction rules between ghosts and gravitons. We also implement a realisation
of a higher derivative gauge fixing term for quadratic gravity. Secondly, we
implement Feynman rules for Cheung-Remmen variables. These variables present
the general relativity action in a polynomial form and produce a finite set of
Feynman rules. Lastly, we introduce some minor quality-of-life changes to the
package to improve the user experience.

</details>


### [139] [Collective dynamics in holographic fractonic solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17404)
*Ling-Zheng Xia,Lixin Xu,Wei-Jia Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了(3+1)维全息分形体固体模型中的低能集体动力学，发现包括两个声学声子、一个纵向扩散模和一个具有ω∼−ik⁴色散关系的分形亚扩散模在内的多种激发模式。结果表明，分形激发由晶体偶极对称性保护，即使时空对称性被破坏仍保持无能隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索分形物态中受限移动激发的出现机制及其对遍历性破缺的影响，为凝聚态物理中的新奇物态提供理论基础。

Method: 采用(3+1)维全息模型，通过计算黑洞的准正规模来系统研究边界上的低能集体激发行为。

Result: 发现了四种边界水动力激发：两个声学声子、一个纵向扩散模和一个分形亚扩散模（ω∼−ik⁴）；分形模在平移对称性显式破缺下仍保持无能隙。

Conclusion: 分形激发本质上受晶体偶极对称性保护，其存在不依赖于时空对称性的完整，表明该类激发具有鲁棒性和基本对称性起源。

Abstract: Fractonic phases of matter, a class of states in which collective excitations
with constrained mobility exist, have recently emerged as a novel avenue for
ergodicity breaking and garnered broad interest in condensed matter physics. In
this work, we consider a (3+1)-dimensional holographic model of fractonic
solids and investigate the low-energy collective dynamics systematically. By
computing the quasinormal modes of black holes, we obtain all the hydrodynamic
excitations on the boundary, including two acoustic phonons, a longitudinal
diffusive mode as well as a fractonic subdiffusive mode with the dispersion
$\omega \sim-ik^4$. In addition, it is found that the fracton mode remains
gapless when translational symmetry is explicitly broken. These results suggest
that fractonic excitations are inherently protected by the crystal-dipole
symmetry in solids and are qualitatively unaffected by broken spacetime
symmetries.

</details>


### [140] [The Spectrum-generating Algebra for Bosonic Strings in a Linear Dilaton Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17411)
*Dripto Biswas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将玻色DDF算符的系统构造推广到光锥线性膨胀背景，研究高自旋弦态在非平直时空中的行为。结果表明，谱生成代数与平直时空情况同构，仅存在一些细微差异，并自然地体现在谱和变形的动量守恒（非守恒）δ函数中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高自旋弦态在非平直时空中的行为，特别是在可解的非平凡弦背景下研究高自旋相互作用。

Method: 推广玻色DDF算符的系统构造至光锥线性膨胀背景，并利用已有结果分析谱生成代数的结构。

Result: 谱生成代数与平直时空情况基本同构，仅存在少数细微差别；大多数推导结果与平直背景相似，修正项在谱和动量（非）守恒δ函数中自然出现。

Conclusion: 该扩展为研究非平凡但精确可解背景下的高自旋相互作用提供了可控框架，揭示了背景几何对弦谱结构的微妙影响。

Abstract: We extend the systematic construction of bosonic DDF operators to the
light-like linear dilaton background to investigate how higher-spin string
states behave beyond flat spacetime. Using previous results, we show that the
spectrum-generating algebra is isomorphic to the flat case up to a few
subtleties. This extension provides a controlled setting to explore higher-spin
interactions in a nontrivial yet exactly solvable string background. Most of
the derivations lead to expressions very similar to those in the flat
background, with the expected modifications appearing quite naturally in the
spectrum and the deformed momentum-(non)conserving delta function.

### [141] [Radiation Entropy in asymptotically AdS Black Holes within f(Q) Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17528)
*Yipeng Liu,Wei Xu,Baocheng Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究在f(Q)引力中渐近AdS黑洞背景下的辐射熵，发现广义熵的面积项需修正，导致岛屿规则被修正；在永恒和坍缩黑洞情形下，辐射熵受f(Q)模型选择影响，信息被编码在最终辐射熵中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索f(Q)引力框架下黑洞辐射熵的行为，检验岛屿规则在非广义相对论理论中的适用性，并揭示引力模型对信息悖论的影响。

Method: 基于欧几里得作用量分析，修正广义熵的面积项，提出修正的岛屿规则，并应用于计算永恒黑洞和坍缩黑洞的辐射熵。

Result: 在永恒黑洞情况下，辐射熵时间独立但随截断面外移而发散，表明s波近似失效；在坍缩黑洞情况下，辐射熵由面积项主导，含与面积成正比的对数修正，符合量子引力预测；辐射熵和Page时间均受f(Q)模型选择影响。

Conclusion: f(Q)引力中的辐射熵行为依赖于具体模型，修正的岛屿规则揭示了引力理论细节对黑洞信息问题的重要影响。

Abstract: We employ the island rule to study the radiation entropy in the background of
asymptotically AdS black holes within f(Q) gravity. Through an analysis based
on the Euclidean action, we find that within this framework the area term of
the generalized entropy must be modified, leading to a corrected island rule.
Using this rule to compute the radiation entropy in the eternal case shows
that, although the result is time-independent, it diverges as the cutoff
surface moves outward, indicating the breakdown of the s-wave approximation.
For a collapsing black hole, the radiation entropy is dominated by the area
term, with a logarithmic correction proportional to the area, which is
consistent with the predictions of quantum gravity theories. Furthermore, both
the radiation entropy and the Page time are ultimately influenced by the choice
of the f(Q) model, implying that information about the underlying gravitational
model is encoded in the final radiation entropy.

</details>


### [142] [On the equivalence of first and second order formulations of the Einstein-Hilbert theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17615)
*F. T. Brandt,J. Frenkel,S. Martins-Filho,D. G. C. McKeon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 证明了爱因斯坦-希尔伯特理论在量子层面上两种背景场表述的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立不同表述之间的等价性以增强理论一致性。

Method: 推导背景有效作用量之间的一般关系，并在一般背景规范下进行显式的一圈计算。

Result: 在一圈阶上验证了对应抵消项拉格朗日量的等价性。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-希尔伯特理论的两种背景场表述在量子层面是等价的。

Abstract: We derive a general relation between the background effective actions, which
directly proves that the two formulations of the Einstein-Hilbert theory with
background fields are equivalent at the quantum level. This basic result has
been substantiated in a general background gauge, by explicit calculations at
one-loop order of the corresponding counterterm Lagrangians.

</details>


### [143] [Matrix Correlators as Discrete Volumes of Moduli Space I: Recursion Relations, the BMN-limit and DSSYK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.17728)
*Alessandro Giacchetto,Pronobesh Maity,Edward A. Mazenc*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文展示了通用单矩阵模型中的某些关联函数定义了黎曼曲面模空间的“离散”体积，推广了随机矩阵与JT引力之间的联系，并证明其满足离散的、类似Mirzakhani的递推关系。在大迹的BMN类极限下，该递推关系趋于连续，关联函数渐近于Kontsevich体积。此外，文章证明DSSYK的ETH矩阵积分为Weil-Petersson体积提供了一个离散的q-模拟，证实了Okuyama的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索随机矩阵模型与量子引力、模空间体积之间的深层联系，推广已知的连续结构至离散情形，并验证关于DSSYK模型中q-模拟体积的猜想。

Method: 通过研究远离双标度极限的矩阵积分，引入离散体积概念；利用BMN-like极限分析其向连续情形的过渡；结合ETH矩阵积分处理DSSYK模型，建立q-模拟与Weil-Petersson体积的关系。

Result: 发现了矩阵模型中关联函数对应于离散模空间体积；证明其满足离散Mirzakhani型递推；在极限下恢复Kontsevich体积；并证明DSSYK的ETH积分给出Weil-Petersson体积的q-模拟。

Conclusion: 单矩阵模型可自然导出离散化的模空间体积，且具有普适递推结构，在适当极限下连接经典结果，同时为DSSYK理论提供了对Okuyama猜想的严格证明。

Abstract: We show certain correlators in generic one-matrix models define a notion of
``discrete'' volumes of the moduli space of Riemann surfaces, generalizing the
connection between random matrices and JT gravity. We prove they obey a
discrete, Mirzakhani-like recursion relation. Their fundamental discreteness
crucially relies upon studying these matrix integrals away from the usual
double-scaling limit. In a BMN-like limit of large traces, this recursion
universally goes over to a continuous one, and the correlators asymptote to the
volumes of Kontsevich. Finally, we demonstrate that the ETH matrix integral for
DSSYK furnishes a discrete, $q$-analog of the Weil--Petersson volumes, thereby
proving a conjecture due to K. Okuyama.

</details>
